        var activeSheetId;

        function switchToSheet(id) {
          if (document.getElementById('sheet-menu')) {
            document.getElementById('sheet-button-' + activeSheetId)
                .className = '';
            document.getElementById('sheet-button-' + id).className = 'active';
          }

          document.getElementById(activeSheetId).style.display = 'none';
          document.getElementById(id).style.display = '';
          activeSheetId = id;

          // posObjs() is defined in embeddedObjectJs (see EmbeddedObjectHtmlBuilder.java)
          posObjs();
          return false;
        }
        
        function init() {
        var optPageSwitcher;
        
        function resize() {
          var optTopBar = document.getElementById('top-bar');
          var adjustedHeight = window.innerHeight - (optTopBar ? optTopBar.offsetHeight : 0);
          var adjustedWidth = window.innerWidth;
          var sheetsViewport = document.getElementById('sheets-viewport');
          sheetsViewport.style.width = (adjustedWidth + 'px');
          sheetsViewport.style.height = (adjustedHeight + 'px');
          if (optPageSwitcher) {
            optPageSwitcher.resize(adjustedWidth, adjustedHeight);
          }
        }
        resize();
        window.onresize = resize;
        }

The &quot;Direct Link&quot; goes to a web page containing a list of advisors that need to be crawled. The &quot;Import.IO Links&quot; goes to a dataset at Import.IO that crawls the web pages of those advisors. The &quot;Extractor Links&quot; goes to an extractor that grabs ONLY the links  from the &quot;Direct Link&quot; page. </td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R9" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">10</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R10" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">11</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr" colspan="7">NOTE: The &quot;Extractor Links&quot; is only necessary IF the &quot;Import.IO Links&quot; is a crawler. If an extractor was used to grab the advisor&#39;s data, then the &quot;Extractor Links&quot; column must be left blank.</td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R11" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">12</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R12" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">13</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr">2</td><td class="s0" dir="ltr" colspan="6">Please do not shorthand any of the names. So, please type out &quot;Harvard University&quot; instead of &quot;Harvard&quot;. This rule applies to all school and department names as well.</td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R13" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">14</div></th><td class="s1" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R14" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">15</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr">3</td><td class="s0" dir="ltr" colspan="6">The resource column should have one of the following four words:</td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R15" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">16</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s4" dir="ltr">advisor</td><td class="s4" dir="ltr">course</td><td class="s4" dir="ltr">thesis</td><td class="s4" dir="ltr">funding</td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R16" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">17</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s1" dir="ltr" colspan="6">depending on the type of resource information the Import.IO crawler returns.</td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R17" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">18</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R18" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">19</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr">4</td><td class="s5" dir="ltr" colspan="6">Each resource has specific information that needs to be placed into the database:</td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R19" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">20</div></th><td class="s6" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s7" dir="ltr">Advisor:</td><td class="s5" dir="ltr">Name</td><td class="s5" dir="ltr">Header</td><td class="s5" dir="ltr">Info</td><td class="s5" dir="ltr">Block</td><td class="s8" dir="ltr"></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R20" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">21</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr" colspan="9">&quot;Header&quot; is a descriptive sentence about the advisor. &quot;Professor of Sociology&quot; is a good example. </td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R21" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">22</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr" colspan="9">&quot;Info&quot; is a block of contact information about the advisor. This may include email, phone number, office location, office hours, etc.</td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R22" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">23</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s5" dir="ltr" colspan="9">&quot;Block&quot; is a large block of text describing the advisor. This is usually the advisor&#39;s bio, but it can be a list of achievements and other relevant information.</td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R23" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">24</div></th><td class="s6" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s7" dir="ltr">Course:</td><td class="s5" dir="ltr">Name</td><td class="s5" dir="ltr">Header</td><td class="s5" dir="ltr">Block</td><td class="s5" dir="ltr">Faculty</td><td class="s5" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s5" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s5" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s8" dir="ltr"></td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R24" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">25</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr" colspan="9">&quot;Block&quot; is a block of text about the course</td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R25" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">26</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr" colspan="9">&quot;Faculty&quot; is the name(s) of professor(s) who teach and/or run the course</td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R26" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">27</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr" colspan="9">&quot;Name&quot; is the title of the course</td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R27" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">28</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s5" dir="ltr" colspan="9">If there are multiple departments in a scraper, then leave the Department column in the SPREADSHEET blank and enter a Department column in the SCRAPER instead.</td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R28" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">29</div></th><td class="s6" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s7" dir="ltr">Thesis:</td><td class="s5" dir="ltr">Title</td><td class="s5" dir="ltr">Name</td><td class="s5" dir="ltr">Advisor</td><td class="s5" dir="ltr">Abstract</td><td class="s5" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s5" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s5" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s8" dir="ltr"></td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R29" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">30</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr" colspan="9">&quot;Title&quot; is the title of the thesis</td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R30" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">31</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr" colspan="9">&quot;Name&quot; is the name of the writer of the thesis</td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R31" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">32</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr" colspan="9">&quot;Advisor&quot; is the name of the advisor who helped the author write their thesis</td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R32" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">33</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s5" dir="ltr" colspan="9">&quot;Abstract&quot; is the abstract or description of the thesis</td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R33" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">34</div></th><td class="s6" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s7" dir="ltr">Funding:</td><td class="s5" dir="ltr">Name</td><td class="s5" dir="ltr">Info</td><td class="s5" dir="ltr">Link</td><td class="s5" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s5" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s5" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s5" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s8" dir="ltr"></td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R34" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">35</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr" colspan="9">&quot;Name&quot; is the title of the grant or funding source</td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R35" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">36</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr" colspan="9">&quot;Info&quot; is the description and/or requirements of the grant</td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R36" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">37</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr" colspan="9">&quot;Link&quot; is the URL that goes to a web page or form with more information about the grant or funding source</td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R37" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">38</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R38" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">39</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr" colspan="9">All crawlers MUST have this information with these exact labels. Otherwise, the information will not be saved properly.</td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R39" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">40</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R40" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">41</div></th><td class="s0" dir="ltr">5</td><td class="s9" dir="ltr" colspan="8">If you come across a website (or web page) that must be manually crawled, then note this in the spreadsheet by placing the word &quot;manual&quot; in the space for the Import.IO link. For example:</td><td class="s0" dir="ltr"></td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R41" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">42</div></th><td class="s10"></td><td class="s11" dir="ltr">University</td><td class="s11" dir="ltr">School</td><td class="s11" dir="ltr">Department</td><td class="s11" dir="ltr">Resource Type</td><td class="s11" dir="ltr">Direct Links</td><td class="s12" dir="ltr">Import.IO Link</td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr style='height:21px;'><th id="1852672240R42" style="height: 21px;" class="row-headers-background row-header-shim"><div class="row-header-wrapper" style="line-height: 21px;">43</div></th><td class="s10"></td><td class="s13" dir="ltr">Harvard University</td><td class="s13" dir="ltr">Divinity School</td><td class="s13" dir="ltr">Divinity</td><td class="s13" dir="ltr">advisor</td><td class="s14 softmerge"><div class="softmerge-inner" style="width: 114px; <script type='text/javascript'>
function posObj(sheet, id, row, col, x, y) {
  var r = document.getElementById(sheet+'R'+row);
  var c = document.getElementById(sheet+'C'+col);
  if (r && c) {
    var s = document.getElementById(id).style;
    var t = y;
    while (r) {
      t += r.offsetTop;
      r = r.offsetParent;
    }
    var l = x;
    while (c) {
      l += c.offsetLeft;
      c = c.offsetParent;
    }
    s.left = l + 'px';
    s.top = t + 'px';
    s.display = 'block';
    s.border = '1px solid #000000';
  }
};
function posObjs() {
};
posObjs();</script>
